<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeven.html>zeven</a> (766)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sēven</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sivun</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sivon</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sebun</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> earlier <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sebunt</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*septḿ̥</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <i>-t</i> added <a href = vnd.unilang:through.html>through</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:influence.html>influence</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:nine.html>nine</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:ten.html>ten</a>".
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral"><a href = vnd.unilang:numeral.html>Numeral</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeven.html>zeven</a></strong>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:seven.html>seven</a></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sēven</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeef.html>zeef</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeven.html>zeven</a></strong>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zier.html>zier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zier.html>ziertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijd.html>zijd</a> (71584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijt.html>zijt</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sijt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wide.html>wide</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:broad.html>broad</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sīd</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sīdaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ample.html>ample</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijd.html>zijd</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">zijder</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">zijdst</b>)

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></strong>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:archaic.html>archaic</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:standard.html>standard</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wezen.html>wezen</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:standard.html>standard</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bennen</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sijn</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sīn</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:originally.html>originally</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> reflexive <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sīnaz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*seyno-</i>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:sein.html>sein</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:sin.html>sin</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>Ultimately</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> Proto-Indo-European reflexive pronoun <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*swe</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:related.html>related</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> Russian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">себя</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sebja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">suus</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἑός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">heós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:etc.html>etc</a>.
</p>
